  13              	;@"      The SOURCE CODE is distributed "AS IS" WITHOUT WARRANTIES AS TO    "
  14              	;@"   PERFORMANCE OF MERCHANTABILITY WHETHER EXPRESSED OR IMPLIED.          "

  17              	;@"																			"
  18              	;@"*************************************************************************"
  19              	;@"                                                                         "
  20              	;@"       This code expands on my earlier SmartStart bootstub assembler for "
  21              	;@" the Pi3. It directly supports multicore operation in C/C++. To do that  "
  22              	;@" it provides stack space to each core and provides a modified bootloader "
  23              	;@" spinlock that protects against registers X0-X7 trashed. As any C/C++    "
  24              	;@" 64 bit compiler will trash those registers, to use C/C++ in multicore   "
  25              	;@" programming this protection must be done.								"
  26              	;@"       This is a matching paired AARCH64 stub for the 64bit linker file  "
  27              	;@" and carries the samme arrangement as AARCH32 to ease porting.		    "
  28              	;@"																            "
  29              	;@"+++++++++++++++++++++++[ REVISIONS ]+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++"
  30              	;@"  1.01 Initial release .. Pi autodetection main aim                      "
  31              	;@"  1.02 Many functions moved out C to aide 32/64 bit compatability        "
  32              	;@"  2.01 Futher reductions to bare minmum assembeler code                  "
  33              	;@"  2.02 Multicore functionality added                                     "
  34              	;@"  2.03 Timer Irq support added  											"
  35              	;@"+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++"*/
  36              	
  37              	.section ".text.startup", "ax", %progbits

 127              	//"================================================================"
 128              	    /*  RES1 bits (29,28,23,22,20,11) to 1
 129              		 *  RES0 bits (31,30,27,21,17,13,10,6) +
 130              		 *  UCI,EE,EOE,WXN,nTWE,nTWI,UCT,DZE,I,UMA,SED,ITD,
 131              		 *  CP15BEN,SA0,SA,C,A,M to 0 */

 135 00e8 000074B2 		orr    x0, x0, #(0x1 << 12)           // The I bit on (instruction cache)
 136 00ec 001018D5 		msr	sctlr_el1, x0

 144 00fc 20401CD5 		msr	elr_el2, x0							// Set elevated return register
 145 0100 E0039FD6 		eret									// Call elevated return
 146              	exit_el1:

 150

 153              	//"================================================================"
 154 0110 C1050058 		ldr x1, =RPi_CoresReady					// Address of CoreReady count

 157 011c 200000B9 		str w0, [x1]							// Update CoreReady count

 170 012c E3080058 		ldr x3, =__bss_end__

 181              	//			Core0 will bring Core 1,2,3 to secondary spin

 183              	#define spin_cpu1 0xe0

 185 014c 62080058 		ldr x2, =multicore_start				// Function we are going to call
 186 0150 220000F9 		str	x2, [x1]							// Store the function address to core1

 228              	/*++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++}
 229              	{    Modified bootloader Spin loop but tolerant on registers X0-X7 for C    }
 230              	{++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++*/
 231              	#define spin_cpu0 0xd8
 232              	.balign	4
 233              	StartSecondarySpin:
 234 0260 A60038D5 		mrs x6, MPIDR_EL1						// Fetch core Id
 235 0264 C6044092 		and x6, x6, #0x3						// Create 2 bit mask of core Id
 236 0268 051B80D2 		mov x5, #spin_cpu0						// Load address of spins
 237 026c 010080D2 		mov x1, #0                              // zero x1 register
 238 0270 A17826F8 		str x1, [x5, x6, lsl #3]				// Make sure caller address is zeroed
 239              	secondary_spin:

 241 0278 A47866F8 	    ldr x4, [x5, x6, lsl #3]				// Fetch address that has been set
 242 027c C4FFFFB4 		cbz x4, secondary_spin					// If zero spin
 243 0280 000080D2 		mov x0, #0

 248 0294 80003FD6 		blr x4									// Call the function set
 249 0298 F2FFFF17 		b StartSecondarySpin					// Loop back to spinlock
 250
